<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:directly.html>directly</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">grotta</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> indirectly <a href = vnd.unilang:via.html>via</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language"><a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">grotte</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">crypta</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek"><a href = vnd.unilang:ancient.html>Ancient</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:greek.html>Greek</a></a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κρυπτός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kruptós</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. ***grut.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:grut.html>grut</a> (51772)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">grutte</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gurte</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*grutti</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*grutją</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grut.html>grut</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grutten.html>grutten</a></b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:diminutive.html>diminutive</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grut.html>grutje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">countable <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">groat</span>, broken-up <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> grinded <a href = vnd.unilang:grain.html>grain</a></li>

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">gile</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anglo-Norman_language" class="extiw" title="w:Anglo-Norman language">Anglo-Norman</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">gile</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:guile.html>guile</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">deception</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span><sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Frankish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Frankish language">Frankish</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*wigila</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:ruse.html>ruse</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
